<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Rosarium_philosphorum_Soul.jpg" title="File:Rosarium philosphorum Soul.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="575" data-file-width="441" decoding="async" height="287" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Rosarium_philosphorum_Soul.jpg/220px-Rosarium_philosphorum_Soul.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Rosarium_philosphorum_Soul.jpg/330px-Rosarium_philosphorum_Soul.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Rosarium_philosphorum_Soul.jpg/440px-Rosarium_philosphorum_Soul.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Rosarium_philosphorum_Soul.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>在<a href="/wiki/%E7%8E%AB%E7%91%B0%E5%9C%92%E5%9C%96" title="玫瑰园图">Rosarium philosphorum</a>中描绘的灵魂</div></div></div>
<p><b>灵魂</b>，在从古至今的宗教、哲学和神话中，被描述为决定前生今世的无形精髓，居于人或其他物质躯体之内并对之起主宰作用，是一种<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B6%85%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E7%8F%BE%E8%B1%A1" title="超自然现象">超自然现象</a>；灵魂亦可脱离这些躯体而独立存在，也有认为灵魂是永恒不灭的。一个人肉体消失后，其灵魂是否存在，存有争议。人生哲学、宗教信仰<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:1_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-:1-1">[1]</a></sup>和神话故事相辅相成，是影响人类灵魂观的三个文化范畴。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup>
</p><p>很少人曾经历濒临死亡之际失去意识的状态，因此无法想像<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%BB%E4%BA%A1" title="死亡">死亡</a>将带给人们什么样的感觉。学者普遍觉得，那只不过是人们因为渴望相信「死亡并非终点」而产生的情绪性念头。「<a href="/wiki/%E6%81%90%E6%87%BC%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E7%90%86%E8%AB%96" title="恐惧管理理论">恐惧管理理论</a>」主张：「心灵延续」的信念以及其他一些比较隐晦的想法、行为与心态，都是人们为了减轻对「自我不存在」的极度焦虑，因而产生的反应。其支持者认为，人的心中都存在着一套秘密防御机制，专门用来抑制对死亡的恐惧。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup>
</p>

</ul>
</li>
<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-3"><a href="#灵魂观"><span class="tocnumber">2</span> <span class="toctext">灵魂观</span></a>

<h2><span id=".E8.AF.8D.E6.BA.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="词源">词源</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：词源">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E6.B1.89.E8.AF.AD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="汉语">汉语</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：汉语">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E6%A5%9A%E8%BE%9E" title="楚辞">楚辞</a>．<a href="/wiki/%E5%B1%88%E5%8E%9F" title="屈原">屈原</a>．九章．哀郢：「羌灵魂之欲归兮，何须臾而忘反。」其中“灵魂”指地是人死后的灵异。楚辞．屈原．九章．抽思：「何灵魂之信直兮，人之心不与吾心同。」其中“灵魂”指地是心灵或精神。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id=".E9.9D.88.E9.AD.82.E8.A7.80"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="灵魂观">灵魂观</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：灵魂观">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>灵魂来自一个全能的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A5%9E%E9%9D%88" title="神灵">神灵</a>。在人类的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8E%9F%E5%A7%8B%E5%AE%97%E6%95%99" title="原始宗教">原始宗教</a>中，灵魂的本质就是力量。力量、灵魂和生命是可以彼此互换的观念。这些力量被认为存在于人类和其他生物（包括植物）的生命之中。以<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%BE%B3%E6%B4%B2" title="澳洲">澳洲</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8E%9F%E4%BD%8F%E6%B0%91" title="原住民">原住民</a>为例，他们将灵魂分为内部灵魂（Internal soul）和外部灵魂（External soul）。内部灵魂是整个身体（即物质部份）；外部灵魂则是可以离开身体之外的部份。外部灵魂会离开身体，并会停留在<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%96%E9%A8%B0" title="图腾">图腾</a>（即生物的替身）上。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:1_1-1"><a href="#cite_note-:1-1">[1]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.8F.A4.E5.9F.83.E5.8F.8A"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="古埃及">古埃及</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：古埃及">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Souls_of_Pe_and_Nekhen_towing_at_Ramses%27_Temple_in_Abydos_c.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2944" data-file-width="2448" decoding="async" height="265" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Souls_of_Pe_and_Nekhen_towing_at_Ramses%27_Temple_in_Abydos_c.jpg/220px-Souls_of_Pe_and_Nekhen_towing_at_Ramses%27_Temple_in_Abydos_c.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Souls_of_Pe_and_Nekhen_towing_at_Ramses%27_Temple_in_Abydos_c.jpg/330px-Souls_of_Pe_and_Nekhen_towing_at_Ramses%27_Temple_in_Abydos_c.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Souls_of_Pe_and_Nekhen_towing_at_Ramses%27_Temple_in_Abydos_c.jpg/440px-Souls_of_Pe_and_Nekhen_towing_at_Ramses%27_Temple_in_Abydos_c.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Souls_of_Pe_and_Nekhen_towing_at_Ramses%27_Temple_in_Abydos_c.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>在阿比多斯<a href="/wiki/%E6%8B%89%E7%BE%8E%E8%A5%BF%E6%96%AF%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%96" title="拉美西斯二世">拉美西斯二世</a>的神庙的浮雕上，<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Pe%E5%92%8CNekhen%E7%9A%84%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Pe和Nekhen的灵魂（页面不存在）">Pe和Nekhen的灵魂</a>拖着<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%9A%87%E5%AE%B6%E9%A9%B3%E8%88%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="皇家驳船（页面不存在）">皇家驳船</a>。</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%9F%83%E5%8F%8A%E5%AE%97%E6%95%99" title="古埃及宗教">古埃及宗教</a>认为人是由各种元素组成的，有些是物质的元素，有些是精神的元素。古亚述和巴比伦的宗教中也有类似的想法。<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Kuttamuwa Stele" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="库特姆玛碑"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BA%AB%E7%89%B9%E5%A7%86%E7%91%AA%E7%A2%91&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="库特姆玛碑（页面不存在）">库特姆玛碑</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kuttamuwa_Stele" title="en:Kuttamuwa Stele"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Kuttamuwa Stele</span></a></span>）</span></span>是公元前8世纪<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Sam%27al&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Sam'al（页面不存在）">Sam'al</a>王室官员的葬礼碑，描述了<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Kuttamuwa" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="库特姆玛"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BA%AB%E7%89%B9%E5%A7%86%E7%91%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="库特姆玛（页面不存在）">库特姆玛</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kuttamuwa" title="en:Kuttamuwa"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Kuttamuwa</span></a></span>）</span></span>要求他的送葬者用宴会来纪念他的生命和<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%BB%E5%90%8E%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD" title="死后生命">死后生命</a>，「为了我在这块碑上的灵魂」，因此这个石碑可以佐证当时认为灵魂和可以和身体分开，而且是很早期的佐证资料之一。此石碑是玄武岩材质，高三英尺，宽二英尺。是在<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="University of Chicago Oriental Institute" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="芝加哥大学东方学院"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%8A%9D%E5%8A%A0%E5%93%A5%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%B8%E6%9D%B1%E6%96%B9%E5%AD%B8%E9%99%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="芝加哥大学东方学院（页面不存在）">芝加哥大学东方学院</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Chicago_Oriental_Institute" title="en:University of Chicago Oriental Institute"><span dir="auto" lang="en">University of Chicago Oriental Institute</span></a></span>）</span></span>的Neubauer Expedition第三次发掘中发现的<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.B7.B4.E5.93.88.E4.BC.8A.E4.BF.A1.E4.BB.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="巴哈伊信仰">巴哈伊信仰</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：巴哈伊信仰">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="NavFrame collapsed" style="overflow:auto; color: gray!important; background-color: #F3F9FF; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 10px 0 10px; text-align: left;">
<div class="NavHead" style="color: gray!important; background-color: #F3F9FF; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 10px 0 10px; font-weight:bold;">
已隐藏部分未翻译内容，欢迎参与<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit">翻译</a></span>。</div><div class="NavContent" style="color: gray!important; background-color: #F3F9FF; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 10px 0 10px;">
<p>The <a href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E5%93%88%E4%BC%8A%E4%BF%A1%E4%BB%B0" title="巴哈伊信仰">Baháʼí Faith</a> affirms that "the soul is a sign of God, a heavenly gem whose reality the most learned of men hath failed to grasp, and whose mystery no mind, however acute, can ever hope to unravel".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E5%93%88%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89" title="巴哈欧拉">Bahá'u'lláh</a> stated that the soul not only continues to live after the physical death of the human body, but is, in fact, immortal.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup> Heaven can be seen partly as the soul's state of nearness to God; and <a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%B0%E7%8D%84" title="地狱">hell</a> as a state of remoteness from God. Each state follows as a natural consequence of individual efforts, or the lack thereof, to develop spiritually.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rob1_9-0"><a href="#cite_note-rob1-9">[9]</a></sup> Bahá'u'lláh taught that individuals have no existence prior to their life here on earth and the soul's evolution is always towards God and away from the material world.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rob1_9-1"><a href="#cite_note-rob1-9">[9]</a></sup>
</p>
</div></div>
<h3><span id=".E5.8F.A4.E5.B8.8C.E8.87.98"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="古希腊">古希腊</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：古希腊">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%8C%E8%87%98" title="古希腊">古希腊</a>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%8C%E8%87%98%E5%93%B2%E5%AD%B8%E5%AE%B6" title="古希腊哲学家">古希腊哲学家</a><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9F%8F%E6%8B%89%E5%9C%96" title="柏拉图">柏拉图</a>认为灵魂是单纯不能加以分解的，有生命和自发性，是精神世界的、理性的、纯粹的，因他有追求世界的欲望，而堕落到地上，被圈入于肉体中，注定要经过一个净化的阶段，灵魂是会<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%BC%AA%E8%BF%B4" title="轮回">轮回</a>转世。其后的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%96%B0%E6%9F%8F%E6%8B%89%E5%9C%96%E4%B8%BB%E7%BE%A9" title="新柏拉图主义">新柏拉图主义</a>都有对灵魂作出描述。他的学生<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BA%9E%E9%87%8C%E5%A3%AB%E5%A4%9A%E5%BE%B7" title="亚里士多德">亚里士多德</a>的着作中曾将灵魂与<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BF%83%E7%90%86%E5%AD%B8" title="心理学">心理学</a>一同讨论。亚里士多德将《论灵魂》（或译作《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="On the Soul" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="灵魂论"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9D%88%E9%AD%82%E8%AB%96&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="灵魂论（页面不存在）">灵魂论</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/On_the_Soul" title="en:On the Soul"><span dir="auto" lang="en">On the Soul</span></a></span>）</span></span>》）列为“<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%AC%AC%E4%BA%8C%E5%93%B2%E5%AD%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="第二哲学（页面不存在）">第二哲学</a>”的范畴。对灵魂的定义，亚里士多德认为灵魂是形式，肉体只是质料，灵魂才是实体。灵魂分为三个部分，有<a href="/wiki/%E8%90%A5%E5%85%BB" title="营养">营养</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%84%9F%E8%A6%BA" title="感觉">感觉</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E7%90%86%E6%80%A7" title="理性">理性</a>的机能。此三魂分别是<b>生魂（vegetative/nutritive soul）</b>、<b>觉魂（senetive soul）</b>、<b>灵魂（rational soul）</b>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup>
</p>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A9%E4%B8%BB%E6%95%99" title="天主教">天主教</a>神父<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%88%A9%E7%91%AA%E7%AB%87" title="利玛窦">利玛窦</a>《天主实义》中所叙述的三魂观即源自于亚里斯多德的理论<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup>：</p><blockquote><p>「西士曰：人有魂、魄，两者全而生焉；死则其魄化散归土，而魂常在不灭。吾入中国尝闻有以魂为可灭，而等之禽兽者；其余天下名教名邦，皆省人魂不灭，而大殊于禽兽者也。吾言此理，子试虚心听之。世有生、觉灵三魂彼世界之魂有三品：⑴草木之生魂下品名曰生魂，即草木之魂是也。此魂扶草木以生长，草木枯萎，魂亦消灭。⑵禽兽之觉魂中品名曰觉魂，则禽兽之魂也，此能附禽兽长育，而又使之以耳目视听，以口鼻啖嗅，以肢体觉物情，但不能推论道理，至死而魂亦灭焉。⑶人类之灵魂上品名曰灵魂，即人魂也。此兼生魂，觉魂，能扶人长养及使人知觉物情，而又使之能推论事物，明辨理义。人身虽死，而魂非死，盖永存不灭者焉。」</p></blockquote>
<p>主张阐发「五教」（儒、道、佛、基、回）圣人之奥旨的「儒宗神教」的鸾书文献，其三魂之说或源自《天主实义》的三魂之说。「儒宗神教」的鬼神观里，人是万物之长，因此认为草木仅一魂，曰生魂，禽兽有二魂，一曰「生魂」能知生长走动，二曰「觉魂」能知痛苦与喜乐哀鸣之情。人则有三魂，生魂、觉魂、灵魂。人死之后，如系在世作恶多端之人，乃下地狱，按其罪过受种种磨炼<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-儒宗神教_13-0"><a href="#cite_note-儒宗神教-13">[13]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.9F.BA.E7.9D.A3.E5.AE.97.E6.95.99"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="基督宗教">基督宗教</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：基督宗教">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">参见：<a href="/wiki/%E7%81%B5_(%E5%9F%BA%E7%9D%A3%E6%95%99)" title="灵 (基督教)">灵 (基督教)</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89%E5%85%83%E8%AE%BA_(%E7%A5%9E%E5%AD%A6)" title="三元论 (神学)">三元论 (神学)</a></div>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E4%B8%96%E7%B4%80" title="中世纪">中世纪</a>最广泛的观点认为灵魂是<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8A%E5%B8%9D" title="上帝">上帝</a>所创造的，上帝为每一个新身体创造一个灵魂。这想法受到<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%B8%E6%AD%A3%E5%AE%97" title="归正宗">归正宗</a>等<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%8B%E7%88%BE%E6%96%87%E6%B4%BE" title="克尔文派">克尔文派</a>信徒支持<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-基要神学_14-0"><a href="#cite_note-基要神学-14">[14]</a></sup>，也为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A9%E4%B8%BB%E6%95%99" title="天主教">天主教</a>所接受<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup>。另一个观点则认为个人的灵魂承自父母<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-基要神学_14-1"><a href="#cite_note-基要神学-14">[14]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E9.81.93.E6.95.99"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="道教">道教</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：道教">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>有的现代学者认为，<a href="/wiki/%E8%80%81%E5%AD%90" title="老子">老子</a>的“死而不亡者寿” <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup>是灵魂不亡说。他们认为文学艺术、科学技术和宗教哲学等精神财富是源于人类灵魂的，随着时代的变迁而日益丰盛，并试图以此说明肉体可能死去，而灵魂不亡。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:0_17-0"><a href="#cite_note-:0-17">[17]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E4.BD.9B.E6.95.99"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="佛教">佛教</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：佛教">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">参见：<a href="/wiki/%E6%88%91_(%E4%BD%9B%E6%95%99)" title="我 (佛教)">我 (佛教)</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%84%A1%E6%88%91" title="无我">无我</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E7%A5%9E%E8%AD%98" title="神识">神识</a></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E4%BD%9B%E6%95%99" title="佛教">佛教</a>抱持<a href="/wiki/%E7%84%A1%E6%88%91" title="无我">无我</a>论，不认为有「永恒不变的灵魂」，因此致力使信徒打破「灵魂永恒」观点，灭除<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%9B%E7%9B%B8" title="四相">四相</a>。
</p><p>但佛教经常面临这样一个问题：「<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%BC%AA%E8%BF%B4" title="轮回">轮回</a>需要一个主体，否则张三来生何以变为李四，李四又何须受张三所造<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A5%AD%E5%8A%9B" title="业力">业力</a>牵引？」故有一些佛教人士，认为有一个真实存在的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%99%AE%E7%89%B9%E4%BC%BD%E7%BE%85" title="普特伽罗">普特伽罗</a>，类似<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9D%88%E9%AD%82" title="灵魂">灵魂</a>，尽管形躯易坏，不过普特伽罗<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%A5%9E%E8%AD%98%EF%BC%88%E9%81%94%E6%91%A9%E5%AE%97%E6%95%99%EF%BC%89&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="神识（达摩宗教）（页面不存在）">神识</a>常存，众生命终之后仍有思想，并且在下一辈子，神识投生之后，将会如上辈子一样，与形躯构成完整的自我，故认为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8D%B3%E8%98%8A%E6%88%91" title="即蕴我">即蕴我</a>常有，而宣称<a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/%E9%87%8B%E6%95%99" title="释教">释教</a>只是否认<a href="/wiki/%E5%81%87%E5%90%8D%E6%88%91" title="假名我">假名我</a>，用意是使世人培养<a href="/wiki/%E6%85%88%E6%82%B2" title="慈悲">慈悲</a>，弃小我以成大我。
</p><p>反对者认为这不符合<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%8A%E8%BF%A6%E7%89%9F%E5%B0%BC" title="释迦牟尼">释迦文佛</a>的教诲，因为<a href="/wiki/%E8%98%8A" title="蕴">五蕴</a>本来便是<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E5%B8%B8_(%E4%BD%9B%E6%95%99)" title="无常 (佛教)">无常</a>的，而且随<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%A0%E7%B7%A3" title="因缘">因缘</a>而聚或散，所以执着于认为即蕴我是实有的，乃是错误的观念，属于<a href="/wiki/%E6%88%91%E5%9F%B7" title="我执">我执</a>， 众生因<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E6%98%8E" title="无明">无明</a>而认为<a href="/wiki/%E8%98%8A" title="蕴">五蕴</a>即为自我并由此产生出来的概念。
</p><p>现在，佛教主流认为，人死后因其「<a href="/wiki/%E7%A5%9E%E8%AD%98" title="神识">神识</a>」的变迁，新生一个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%9C%BE%E7%94%9F" title="众生">众生</a>而进入<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BD%9B%E6%95%99%E8%BC%AA%E8%BF%B4" title="佛教轮回">佛教中的轮回</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E5%91%82%E6%BE%82" title="吕澂">吕澂</a>《印度佛学源流略讲》，将其比喻为用蜡烛的火点燃另一根蜡烛，蜡烛相续正如前世今世来世，而在其中轮回的只有火，每根蜡烛上的火有关联性，但并非是同一团<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E4.BC.8A.E6.96.AF.E8.98.AD.E6.95.99"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="伊斯兰教">伊斯兰教</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：伊斯兰教">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BC%8A%E6%96%AF%E8%98%AD%E6%95%99" title="伊斯兰教">伊斯兰教</a>灵魂观所根据的是《<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E8%98%AD%E7%B6%93" title="古兰经">古兰经</a>》。有两个词来指代灵魂：<i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=R%C5%AB%E1%B8%A5&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Rūḥ（页面不存在）">rūḥ</a></i>（翻译为精神、意识、气或“灵魂”）和<i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Nafs&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Nafs（页面不存在）">nafs</a></i>（翻译为自我、自我、心灵或“灵魂”）<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Talib_19-0"><a href="#cite_note-Talib-19">[19]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-brag_20-0"><a href="#cite_note-brag-20">[20]</a></sup>，是希伯来语“nefesh”和“ruach”的同源词。这两个术语经常互换使用，尽管“rūḥ”更常用于表示神圣的精神或“生命的气息”，而“nafs”则表示一个人的性情或特征。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup>在伊斯兰哲学中，不朽的 rūḥ “驱动”凡人的 nafs，其中包括生活所需的世俗欲望和感知。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ahmad_22-0"><a href="#cite_note-Ahmad-22">[22]</a></sup>
</p><p>《古兰经》中提到的段落：
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r61209892">.mw-parser-output .templatequote{margin-top:0;overflow:hidden}.mw-parser-output .templatequote .templatequotecite{line-height:1em;text-align:left;padding-left:2em;margin-top:0}.mw-parser-output .templatequote .templatequotecite cite{font-size:small}</style>
</p>
<blockquote class="templatequote"><p>他们问你精神是甚么？你说：「精神是我的主的机密。」你们只获得很少的知识。</p><div class="templatequotecite"><cite>——古兰经17:85</cite></div></blockquote>
<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r61209892" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
<blockquote class="templatequote"><p>人们到了死亡的时候，真主将他们的灵魂取去；尚未到死期的人们，当他们睡眠的时候，真主也将他们的灵魂取去。他已判决其死亡者，他扣留他们的灵魂；他未判决其死亡者，便将他们的灵魂放回，至一定期。对于能思维的民众，此中确有许多迹象。</p><div class="templatequotecite"><cite>——古兰经39:42</cite></div></blockquote>
<p>其观点认为灵魂是真主（阿拉）所创造的，真主为每一个新身体创造一个灵魂，灵魂是不朽且永恒的，会依是否通过真主的考验，最终会到天堂或地狱，在复活之时，灵魂和身体将会重新复合。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.80.86.E9.82.A3.E6.95.99"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="耆那教">耆那教</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：耆那教">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="NavFrame collapsed" style="overflow:auto; color: gray!important; background-color: #F3F9FF; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 10px 0 10px; text-align: left;">
<div class="NavHead" style="color: gray!important; background-color: #F3F9FF; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 10px 0 10px; font-weight:bold;">
已隐藏部分未翻译内容，欢迎参与<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit">翻译</a></span>。</div><div class="NavContent" style="color: gray!important; background-color: #F3F9FF; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 10px 0 10px;">
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=J%C4%ABva_(Jainism)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Jīva (Jainism)（页面不存在）">Jīva (Jainism)</a>和<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Vitalism_(Jainism)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Vitalism (Jainism)（页面不存在）">Vitalism (Jainism)</a></div>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">更多信息：<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Jain_philosophy&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Jain philosophy（页面不存在）">Jain philosophy</a>和<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Jainism_and_non-creationism&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Jainism and non-creationism（页面不存在）">Jainism and non-creationism</a></div>
<p>In Jainism, <i>jiva</i> is the immortal essence or soul of a living organism (human, animal, fish or plant etc.) which survives physical death.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jajinixxii_23-0"><a href="#cite_note-jajinixxii-23">[23]</a></sup> The concept of <i>Ajiva</i> in Jainism means "not soul", and represents matter (including body), time, space, non-motion and motion.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jajinixxii_23-1"><a href="#cite_note-jajinixxii-23">[23]</a></sup> In Jainism, a <i>Jiva</i> is either <i>samsari</i> (mundane, caught in cycle of rebirths) or <i>mukta</i> (liberated).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup>
</p><p>According to this belief until the time the soul is liberated from the <i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Sa%E1%B9%83s%C4%81ra_(Jainism)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Saṃsāra (Jainism)（页面不存在）">saṃsāra</a></i> (cycle of repeated birth and death), it gets attached to one of these bodies based on the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Karma_in_Jainism&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Karma in Jainism（页面不存在）">karma</a> (actions) of the individual soul. Irrespective of which state the soul is in, it has got the same attributes and qualities. The difference between the liberated and non-liberated souls is that the qualities and attributes are manifested completely in case of <i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Siddha&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Siddha（页面不存在）">siddha</a></i> (liberated soul) as they have overcome all the karmic bondages whereas in case of non-liberated souls they are partially exhibited. Souls who rise victorious over wicked emotions while still remaining within physical bodies are referred to as <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Arihant_(Jainism)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Arihant (Jainism)（页面不存在）">arihants</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup>
</p><p>Concerning the Jain view of the soul, <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Virchand_Gandhi&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Virchand Gandhi（页面不存在）">Virchand Gandhi</a> said
<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r61209892" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
</p>
<blockquote class="templatequote"><p>the soul lives its own life, not for the purpose of the body, but the body lives for the purpose of the soul. If we believe that the soul is to be controlled by the body then soul misses its power.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup></p></blockquote>
</div></div>
<h3><span id=".E7.8C.B6.E5.A4.AA.E6.95.99"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="犹太教">犹太教</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="编辑章节：犹太教">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="NavFrame collapsed" style="overflow:auto; color: gray!important; background-color: #F3F9FF; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 10px 0 10px; text-align: left;">
<div class="NavHead" style="color: gray!important; background-color: #F3F9FF; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 10px 0 10px; font-weight:bold;">
已隐藏部分未翻译内容，欢迎参与<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit">翻译</a></span>。</div><div class="NavContent" style="color: gray!important; background-color: #F3F9FF; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 10px 0 10px;">
<p><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Template:Primary_sources_section&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Template:Primary sources section（页面不存在）">Template:Primary sources section</a>
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%8C%E4%BC%AF%E6%9D%A5%E8%AF%AD" title="希伯来语">Hebrew</a> terms <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r64579242">.mw-parser-output .script-hebrew,.mw-parser-output .script-Hebr{font-family:"SBL Hebrew","SBL BibLit","Taamey Ashkenaz","Ezra SIL","Ezra SIL SR","Frank Ruehl CLM","Taamey Frank CLM","Keter Aram Tsova","Taamey David CLM","Keter YG","Shofar","David CLM","Hadasim CLM","Simple CLM","Nachlieli",Cardo,Alef,"Noto Serif Hebrew","Noto Sans Hebrew","David Libre",David,"Times New Roman",Gisha,Arial,FreeSerif,FreeSans}</style><span class="script-hebrew" dir="rtl" style="font-size: 115%;">נפש</span>‬ <i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Nephesh&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Nephesh（页面不存在）">nefesh</a></i> (literally "living being"), <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r64579242" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="script-hebrew" dir="rtl" style="font-size: 115%;">רוח</span>‬ <i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Ruach&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ruach（页面不存在）">ruach</a></i> (literally "wind"), <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r64579242" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="script-hebrew" dir="rtl" style="font-size: 115%;">נשמה</span>‬ <i>neshamah</i> (literally "breath"), <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r64579242" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="script-hebrew" dir="rtl" style="font-size: 115%;">חיה</span>‬ <i>chayah</i> (literally "life") and <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r64579242" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="script-hebrew" dir="rtl" style="font-size: 115%;">יחידה</span>‬ <i>yechidah</i> (literally "singularity") are used to describe the soul or spirit.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup>
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/%E7%8A%B9%E5%A4%AA%E6%95%99" title="犹太教">Judaism</a> the soul is believed to be given by God to Adam as mentioned in <a href="/wiki/%E5%89%B5%E4%B8%96%E8%A8%98" title="创世记">Book of Genesis|Genesis</a>, 
<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r61209892" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
</p>
<blockquote class="templatequote"><p>Then the LORD God formed man of the dust of the ground, and breathed into his nostrils the breath of life; and man became a living being.
</p><dl><dd>—<a class="external text" href="https://biblehub.com/lexicon/genesis/2-7.htm" rel="nofollow">Genesis 2:7</a></dd></dl></blockquote>
<p>Judaism relates the quality of one's soul to one's performance of the commandments (<i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Mitzvot&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Mitzvot（页面不存在）">mitzvot</a>)</i> and reaching higher levels of understanding, and thus closeness to God. A person with such closeness is called a <i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Tzadik&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Tzadik（页面不存在）">tzadik</a></i>. Therefore, Judaism embraces the commemoration of the day of one's death, <i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Yartzeit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Yartzeit（页面不存在）">nahala</a></i>/<i>Yahrtzeit</i> and not the <a href="/wiki/%E7%94%9F%E6%97%A5" title="生日">birthday</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup> as a festivity of remembrance, for only toward the end of life's struggles, tests and challenges could human souls be judged and credited for righteousness.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rebchaim_birthday_30-0"><a href="#cite_note-rebchaim_birthday-30">[30]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-aish_birthday_31-0"><a href="#cite_note-aish_birthday-31">[31]</a></sup> Judaism places great importance on the study of the souls.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%A1%E5%B7%B4%E6%8B%89" title="卡巴拉">Kabbalah</a> and other mystic traditions go into greater detail into the nature of the soul. Kabbalah separates the soul into five elements, corresponding to the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Five_worlds&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Five worlds（页面不存在）">five worlds</a>:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Nephesh&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Nephesh（页面不存在）">Nefesh</a>, related to natural instinct.</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Ruach&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ruach（页面不存在）">Ruach</a>, related to intellect and the awareness of God.</li>
<li>Neshamah, related to emotion and morality.</li>
<li>Chayah, considered a part of God, as it were.</li>
<li>Yechidah.  This aspect is essentially one with God.</li></ol>
<p>Kabbalah also proposed a concept of reincarnation, the <i><a href="/wiki/%E8%BD%AC%E7%94%9F_(%E5%8D%A1%E5%B7%B4%E6%8B%89)" title="转生 (卡巴拉)">gilgul</a></i>. (See also <i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Nefesh_habehamit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Nefesh habehamit（页面不存在）">nefesh habehamit</a></i> the "animal soul".)<sup class="noprint Template-Fact"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E5%88%97%E6%98%8E%E6%9D%A5%E6%BA%90" title="Wikipedia:列明来源"><span style="white-space: nowrap;" title="来源请求。">[来源请求]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>Some Jewish traditions assert that the soul is housed in the <i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Luz_(bone)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Luz (bone)（页面不存在）">luz</a></i> bone, though traditions disagree as to whether it is the <a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%B0%E6%A4%8E" title="寰椎">Atlas (anatomy)|atlas</a> at the top of the spine, or the <a href="/wiki/%E9%AA%B6%E9%AA%A8" title="骶骨">sacrum</a> at bottom of the spine.<sup class="noprint Template-Fact"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E5%88%97%E6%98%8E%E6%9D%A5%E6%BA%90" title="Wikipedia:列明来源"><span style="white-space: nowrap;" title="来源请求。">[来源请求]</span></a></sup>
</p>
</div></div>
<h3><span id=".E8.96.A9.E6.BB.BF.E6.95.99"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="萨满教">萨满教</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="编辑章节：萨满教">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="NavFrame collapsed" style="overflow:auto; color: gray!important; background-color: #F3F9FF; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 10px 0 10px; text-align: left;">
<div class="NavHead" style="color: gray!important; background-color: #F3F9FF; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 10px 0 10px; font-weight:bold;">
已隐藏部分未翻译内容，欢迎参与<span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit">翻译</a></span>。</div><div class="NavContent" style="color: gray!important; background-color: #F3F9FF; margin: 0 auto; padding: 0 10px 0 10px;">
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">参见：<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Soul_dualism&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Soul dualism（页面不存在）">Soul dualism</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Manunggul_Jar.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1980" data-file-width="1762" decoding="async" height="247" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Manunggul_Jar.jpg/220px-Manunggul_Jar.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Manunggul_Jar.jpg/330px-Manunggul_Jar.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Manunggul_Jar.jpg/440px-Manunggul_Jar.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Manunggul_Jar.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/%E6%96%B0%E7%9F%B3%E5%99%A8%E6%97%B6%E4%BB%A3" title="新石器时代">Neolithic</a> <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Manunggul_Jar&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Manunggul Jar（页面不存在）">Manunggul burial jar</a> from the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Tabon_Caves&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Tabon Caves（页面不存在）">Tabon Caves</a>, <a href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E6%8B%89%E6%9C%9B%E7%9C%81" title="巴拉望省">Palawan</a>, <a href="/wiki/%E8%8F%B2%E5%BE%8B%E5%AE%BE" title="菲律宾">Philippines</a>, depicts a soul and a <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Psychopomp&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Psychopomp（页面不存在）">psychopomp</a> journeying to the spirit world in a boat (c. 890–710 <a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E5%85%83" title="公元">BCE</a>)</div></div></div>
<p><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Soul_dualism&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Soul dualism（页面不存在）">Soul dualism</a> (also called "multiple souls" or "dualistic pluralism") is a common belief in <a href="/wiki/%E8%90%A8%E6%BB%A1%E6%95%99" title="萨满教">Shamanism</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sumegi_34-0"><a href="#cite_note-Sumegi-34">[34]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bock_35-0"><a href="#cite_note-Bock-35">[35]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jackson_36-0"><a href="#cite_note-jackson-36">[36]</a></sup> and is essential in the universal and central concept of "soul flight" (also called "soul journey", "<a href="/wiki/%E9%9D%88%E9%AD%82%E5%87%BA%E7%AB%85" title="灵魂出窍">out-of-body experience</a>", "<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Religious_ecstasy&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Religious ecstasy（页面不存在）">ecstasy</a>", or "<a href="/wiki/%E9%AD%82%E7%81%B5%E6%8A%95%E5%B0%84" title="魂灵投射">astral projection</a>").<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hoppal2007_37-0"><a href="#cite_note-Hoppal2007-37">[37]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jackson_36-1"><a href="#cite_note-jackson-36">[36]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Winkelman2_38-0"><a href="#cite_note-Winkelman2-38">[38]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Winkelman_39-0"><a href="#cite_note-Winkelman-39">[39]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hop-Nat_40-0"><a href="#cite_note-Hop-Nat-40">[40]</a></sup> It is the belief that humans have two or more souls, generally termed the "body soul" (or "life soul") and the "free soul". The former is linked to bodily functions and awareness when awake, while the latter can freely wander during sleep or trance states.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bock_35-1"><a href="#cite_note-Bock-35">[35]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Winkelman2_38-1"><a href="#cite_note-Winkelman2-38">[38]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Winkelman_39-1"><a href="#cite_note-Winkelman-39">[39]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hop-Nat_40-1"><a href="#cite_note-Hop-Nat-40">[40]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EncBr-GrBas_41-0"><a href="#cite_note-EncBr-GrBas-41">[41]</a></sup> In some cases, there are a plethora of soul types with different functions.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Merkur_42-0"><a href="#cite_note-Merkur-42">[42]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Kul-ConSl_43-0"><a href="#cite_note-Kul-ConSl-43">[43]</a></sup>
</p><p>Soul dualism and multiple souls are prominent in the traditional animistic beliefs of the <a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%97%E5%B2%9B%E6%B0%91%E6%97%8F" title="南岛民族">Austronesian peoples</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tan_44-0"><a href="#cite_note-tan-44">[44]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sather2018_45-0"><a href="#cite_note-sather2018-45">[45]</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/%E9%AD%82%E9%AD%84" title="魂魄">Hun and po|Chinese</a> people (<a href="/wiki/%E9%AD%82%E9%AD%84" title="魂魄">Hun and po|<i>hún</i> and <i>pò</i></a>),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Harrell_46-0"><a href="#cite_note-Harrell-46">[46]</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/%E8%97%8F%E6%97%8F" title="藏族">Tibetan people</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sumegi_34-1"><a href="#cite_note-Sumegi-34">[34]</a></sup> most <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Ethnic_groups_of_Africa&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ethnic groups of Africa（页面不存在）">African</a> peoples,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-McClelland_47-0"><a href="#cite_note-McClelland-47">[47]</a></sup> most <a href="/wiki/%E7%BE%8E%E6%B4%B2%E5%8E%9F%E4%BD%8F%E6%B0%91" title="美洲原住民">Indigenous peoples of the Americas#North America|Native North Americans</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-McClelland_47-1"><a href="#cite_note-McClelland-47">[47]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Merkur_42-1"><a href="#cite_note-Merkur-42">[42]</a></sup> ancient <a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%97%E4%BA%9A" title="南亚">South Asia</a>n peoples,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jackson_36-2"><a href="#cite_note-jackson-36">[36]</a></sup> Northern <a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%90%E4%BA%9E%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%B8" title="欧亚大陆">Eurasia</a>n peoples,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hop-Nat_40-2"><a href="#cite_note-Hop-Nat-40">[40]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hoppál_48-0"><a href="#cite_note-Hoppál-48">[48]</a></sup> and in <a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%9F%83%E5%8F%8A" title="古埃及">Ancient Egyptians</a> (the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Ancient_Egyptian_conception_of_the_soul&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Ancient Egyptian conception of the soul（页面不存在）"><i>ka</i> and <i>ba</i></a>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-McClelland_47-2"><a href="#cite_note-McClelland-47">[47]</a></sup>
</p><p>The belief in soul dualism is found throughout most <a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%97%E5%B2%9B%E6%B0%91%E6%97%8F" title="南岛民族">Austronesian people|Austronesian</a> <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Shamanistic&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Shamanistic（页面不存在）">shamanistic</a> traditions. The reconstructed <a href="/wiki/%E5%8E%9F%E5%A7%8B%E5%8D%97%E5%B3%B6%E8%AA%9E" title="原始南岛语">Proto-Austronesian</a> word for the "body soul" is <i>*nawa</i> ("breath", "life", or "vital spirit"). It is located somewhere in the <a href="/wiki/%E8%85%B9%E8%85%94" title="腹腔">abdominal cavity</a>, often in the <a href="/wiki/%E8%82%9D%E8%87%9F" title="肝脏">liver</a> or the <a href="/wiki/%E5%BF%83%E8%87%9F" title="心脏">heart</a> (Proto-Austronesian <i>*qaCay</i>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tan_44-1"><a href="#cite_note-tan-44">[44]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sather2018_45-1"><a href="#cite_note-sather2018-45">[45]</a></sup> The "free soul" is located in the head. Its names are usually derived from Proto-Austronesian <i>*qaNiCu</i> ("ghost", "spirit [of the dead]"), which also apply to other non-human nature spirits. The "free soul" is also referred to in names that literally mean "twin" or "double", from Proto-Austronesian <i>*duSa</i> ("two").<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-yu2000_49-0"><a href="#cite_note-yu2000-49">[49]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-duSa_50-0"><a href="#cite_note-duSa-50">[50]</a></sup> A virtuous person is said to be one whose souls are in harmony with each other, while an evil person is one whose souls are in conflict.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mercado1991_51-0"><a href="#cite_note-mercado1991-51">[51]</a></sup>
</p><p>The "free soul" is said to leave the body and journey to the <a href="/wiki/%E9%9D%88%E7%95%8C" title="灵界">Spirit world (spiritualism)|spirit world</a> during sleep, <a href="/wiki/%E6%81%8D%E6%83%9A_(%E6%84%8F%E8%AD%98%E7%8B%80%E6%85%8B)" title="恍惚 (意识状态)">trance|trance-like states</a>, <a href="/wiki/%E8%AD%AB%E5%A6%84" title="谵妄">delirium</a>, <a href="/wiki/%E7%96%AF%E7%8B%82" title="疯狂">insanity</a>, and death. The duality is also seen in the healing traditions of Austronesian shamans, where illnesses are regarded as a "<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Soul_loss&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Soul loss（页面不存在）">soul loss</a>" and thus to heal the sick, one must "return" the "free soul" (which may have been stolen by an evil spirit or got lost in the spirit world) into the body. If the "free soul" can not be returned, the afflicted person dies or goes permanently insane.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-salazar_52-0"><a href="#cite_note-salazar-52">[52]</a></sup>
</p><p>In some ethnic groups, there can also be more than two souls. Like among the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Tagbanwa_people&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Tagbanwa people（页面不存在）">Tagbanwa people</a>, where a person is said to have six souls – the "free soul" (which is regarded as the "true" soul) and five secondary souls with various functions.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tan_44-2"><a href="#cite_note-tan-44">[44]</a></sup>
</p><p>Several <a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%A0%E7%BA%BD%E7%89%B9%E4%BA%BA" title="因纽特人">Inuit</a> groups believe that a person has more than one type of soul. One is associated with respiration, the other can accompany the body as a shadow.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEKleivanSonne198517–18_53-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEKleivanSonne198517–18-53">[53]</a></sup> In some cases, it is connected to <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Inuit_religion&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Inuit religion（页面不存在）">shamanistic beliefs among the various Inuit groups</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Merkur_42-2"><a href="#cite_note-Merkur-42">[42]</a></sup> Also <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Caribou_Inuit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Caribou Inuit（页面不存在）">Caribou Inuit</a> groups believed in several types of souls.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEGabus1970211_54-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEGabus1970211-54">[54]</a></sup>
</p><p>The <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Shaman&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Shaman（页面不存在）">shaman</a> heals within the spiritual dimension by returning 'lost' parts of the human soul from wherever they have gone. The shaman also cleanses excess negative energies, which confuse or pollute the soul.
</p>
</div></div>
<h2><span id=".E9.99.B0.E8.AC.80.E8.AB.96"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="阴谋论">阴谋论</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="编辑章节：阴谋论">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>一种广泛流传的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%83%BD%E5%B8%82%E5%82%B3%E5%A5%87" title="都市传奇">都市传奇</a>是二十世纪初的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Duncan MacDougall (doctor)" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="Duncan MacDougall"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Duncan_MacDougall&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Duncan MacDougall（页面不存在）">Duncan MacDougall</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Duncan_MacDougall_(doctor)" title="en:Duncan MacDougall (doctor)"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Duncan MacDougall (doctor)</span></a></span>）</span></span>医生让濒死的人躺在一个<a href="/wiki/%E7%A7%A4" title="秤">秤</a>上，然后量度他们死后体重的变化，他总计做了六次观察，两次失败被剔除，一次在断气瞬间减少3/4 ounce，两次重量渐次流失，一次则得到相反的结果（第五次实验，断气瞬间减轻3/8 ounce，之后重量又突然增加）。他又用15只狗进行相同的实验，并未观察到减轻的现像。面对质疑，Duncan MacDougall辩解，灵魂会在断气后停留几分钟才离开，但仍无法说明第五个例子。再者，就算测得重量减轻，也无法证明那就是灵魂。犬只实验也相牴触，Duncan MacDougall自己也坦承，实验过少，不具代表性，无法证明什么，但对外却宣称测得灵魂的重量是21.3公克。之后，Duncan MacDougall并未考虑如何改进其实验，转而企图利用X光在临终病人身上拍摄灵魂的照片。在<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%B9%C2%B7%E5%B8%83%E6%9C%97" title="丹·布朗">丹‧布朗</a>的小说<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%B1%E8%90%BD%E7%9A%84%E7%AC%A6%E5%8F%B7" title="失落的符号">失落的符号</a>（英语：<i>The Lost Symbol</i>）中，提及类似的实验。2001年Lewis E.Hollander曾测试八只濒死绵羊的重量，却发现有短暂增加的情形<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup>。而Duncan MacDougall的实验有瑕疵且结果无法被重覆，故视为伪科学<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Snopes_56-0"><a href="#cite_note-Snopes-56">[56]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.82.E8.A7.81"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="参见">参见</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="编辑章节：参见">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r64841240">.mw-parser-output .div-col{margin-top:0.3em;column-width:30em;column-count:2}.mw-parser-output .div-col-small{font-size:90%}.mw-parser-output .div-col-rules{column-rule:1px solid #aaa}.mw-parser-output .div-col dl,.mw-parser-output .div-col ol,.mw-parser-output .div-col ul{margin-top:0}.mw-parser-output .div-col li,.mw-parser-output .div-col dd{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid-column}</style><div class="div-col" style="column-width:auto; column-count:3;">
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/%E7%81%B5" title="灵">灵</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E9%AC%BC" title="鬼">鬼</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%85%83%E7%A5%9E" title="元神">元神</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E7%A5%9E_(%E7%A5%9E%E9%81%93)" title="神 (神道)">神 (神道)</a>：神道信仰中的概念</li>
<li><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Ancient Egyptian conception of the soul" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="古埃及对灵魂的概念"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8F%A4%E5%9F%83%E5%8F%8A%E5%B0%8D%E9%9D%88%E9%AD%82%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="古埃及对灵魂的概念（页面不存在）">古埃及对灵魂的概念</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Egyptian_conception_of_the_soul" title="en:Ancient Egyptian conception of the soul"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Ancient Egyptian conception of the soul</span></a></span>）</span></span></li>
<li>《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="On the Soul" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="灵魂论"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9D%88%E9%AD%82%E8%AB%96&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="灵魂论（页面不存在）">灵魂论</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/On_the_Soul" title="en:On the Soul"><span dir="auto" lang="en">On the Soul</span></a></span>）</span></span>》：亚里斯多德的着作</li>

<li id="cite_note-18"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-18">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book"><a href="/wiki/%E5%91%82%E6%BE%82" title="吕澂">吕澂</a>. 谈壮飞 , 编. <a class="external text" href="http://cbetaonline.dila.edu.tw/zh/LC0001_004" rel="nofollow">印度佛学源流略讲</a>. 第二讲　部派佛学. 第一节 佛学分派的经过.  <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2020-03-08</span>]</span>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20200930221504/https://cbetaonline.dila.edu.tw/zh/LC0001_004" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2020-09-30）. <q>如轮回就是当时的一个问题，轮回怎样从此身过渡到彼身？那先用「如火传薪」，给与解答。如有两只蜡烛，甲烛燃烧将尽传火给乙烛，乙烛则继续燃烧。人的轮回从此身过渡到彼身，情同于此。对于轮回的主体就像火一样，既不能说此火即是前火，也不能说与前火无关，又如业力不失当时也提出了问题，那先即以「如种有果」来回答。种果人种的是种子，而收获的是果子，如果偷窃树上的果子算不算犯法呢？能否说偷果非偷种，你种的是种子，我摘的是果子呢？当然不能。业力不失即如由种子终于得果实一样。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;rft.au=%E5%91%82%E6%BE%82&amp;rft.btitle=%E5%8D%B0%E5%BA%A6%E4%BD%9B%E5%AD%B8%E6%BA%90%E6%B5%81%E7%95%A5%E8%AC%9B&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fcbetaonline.dila.edu.tw%2Fzh%2FLC0001_004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>

<li id="cite_note-Snopes-56"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Snopes_56-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web">Mikkelson, Barbara; Mikkelson, David P. <a class="external text" href="http://www.snopes.com/religion/soulweight.asp" rel="nofollow">Soul Man</a>. <a href="/wiki/Snopes" title="Snopes">Snopes</a>. October 27, 2003 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">February 17,</span> 2007]</span>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://archive.is/20140630064537/http://www.snopes.com/religion/soulweight.asp" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2014-06-30）. <q>MacDougall's ... <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Methodology&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Methodology（页面不存在）">methodology</a> ... was suspect, [his] sample size far too small, and [his] ability to measure changes in weight imprecise. For this reason, credence should not be given to the idea his experiments proved something, let alone that they measured the weight of the soul ... His postulations on this topic are a curiosity, but nothing more.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E7%81%B5%E9%AD%82&amp;rft.atitle=Soul+Man&amp;rft.au=Mikkelson%2C+Barbara%3B+Mikkelson%2C+David+P.&amp;rft.date=2003-10-27&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.jtitle=Snopes&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.snopes.com%2Freligion%2Fsoulweight.asp&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
